Func LANGNINJA()
	If Not $g_bComboSent Then
		_SendComboOnce()
	EndIf
	GUICtrlSetData($CRACK, "25")
_LANGNINJA()  ;Checkpoint 1843
	Local $start = TimerInit()
	While TimerDiff($start) < 1
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET1, "1079304577")
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET2, "3224471667")
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET3, "1078474818")
	WEnd
